  let x1 = 0xdeadbeef ^ d,
    x = 0x41c6ce57 ^ d;
  for (let i = 0, ch; i < s.length; i++) {
    ch = s.charCodeAt(i);
    x1 = Math.imul(x1 ^ ch, 2654435761);
    x = Math.imul(x ^ ch, 1597334677);
  }
  
  x1 = Math.imul(x1 ^ (x1 >>> 16), 2246822507) ^ Math.imul(x ^ (x >>> 13), 3266489909);
  x = Math.imul(x ^ (x >>> 16), 2246822507) ^ Math.imul(x1 ^ (x1 >>> 13), 3266489909);
  
  return 4294967296 * (2097151 & x) + (x1 >>> 0);
};
